    <h1 class="devsite-page-title">
      BigQuery release notes<devsite-actions><devsite-feature-tooltip class="devsite-page-bookmark-tooltip nocontent inline-block" id="devsite-collections-dropdown">

    
    
      <span>
      
      Stay organized with collections
    </span>
    <span>
      
      Save and categorize content based on your preferences.
    </span>
  </devsite-feature-tooltip><!----></devsite-actions>
  
      
    </h1>
  

  <div class="devsite-article-body clearfix
  ">

  
    
    
    
    
    

    <section class="intro">
    

































<p>This page documents production updates to BigQuery. We recommend
that BigQuery developers periodically check this list for any
new announcements. BigQuery automatically updates to the latest
release and cannot be downgraded to a previous version.</p>

<p>For older release notes, see the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/release-notes-archive">Release notes archive</a>.

    </p></section>

    <section>
    
      <p>
        You can see the latest product updates for all of Google Cloud on the
        <a href="/release-notes">
        Google Cloud</a> page, browse and filter all release notes in the
        <a href="https://console.cloud.google.com/release-notes" class="external">Google Cloud console</a>,
        or programmatically access release notes in
        <a class="external" href="https://console.cloud.google.com/bigquery?p=bigquery-public-data&amp;d=google_cloud_release_notes&amp;t=release_notes&amp;page=table">BigQuery</a>.
      </p>
    
    </section>

    <section class="xml">
    
      
      
        
      
      <p>
        To get the latest product updates delivered to you, add the URL of this page to your
        <a href="https://wikipedia.org/wiki/Comparison_of_feed_aggregators" class="external">feed
          reader</a>, or add the
        <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/feeds/bigquery-release-notes.xml">feed URL</a> directly.
      </p>
    
    </section>

    <section class="releases">
      
        

<h2 id="April_07_2026">April 07, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The BigQuery Data Transfer Service now supports incremental data transfers for
the following data source connectors:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/mysql-transfer">MySQL</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/oracle-transfer">Oracle</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/postgresql-transfer">PostgreSQL</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/servicenow-transfer">ServiceNow</a></li>
</ul>

<p>These features are supported in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the built-in text embedding model <code>embeddinggemma-300m</code> in the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-embed"><code>AI.EMBED</code></a>
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-similarity"><code>AI.SIMILARITY</code></a>
functions. This model uses your BigQuery slots to generate embeddings at scale.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_06_2026">April 06, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-agg"><code>AI.AGG</code> function</a>
to semantically aggregate unstructured input data based on natural language
instructions. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use a <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-constraints">custom organization policy</a>
to allow or deny specific operations on these BigQuery resources:
tables, data policies, and row access policies. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_02_2026">April 02, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_connection_statement"><code>CREATE CONNECTION</code></a>,
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#alter_connection_set_options_statement"><code>ALTER CONNECTION SET OPTIONS</code></a>,
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#drop_connection_statement"><code>DROP CONNECTION</code></a>
data definition language (DDL) statements to manage Cloud resource connections
with GoogleSQL. Additionally, you can now use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-control-language#user_list"><code>connection</code> user type</a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-control-language#arguments"><code>PROJECT</code> resource type</a>
with <code>GRANT</code> and <code>REVOKE</code> data control language (DCL) statements to manage
connection and project access. These features are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration/snowflake-migration-intro">BigQuery Migration Service supports SQL translations from Snowflake
SQL to GoogleSQL</a>.
This feature is now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>

<p>With this change, the translation service supports a wider variety of
Snowflake SQL and has improved support for several data types.
Among other changes, the translation service maps Snowflake
<code>INTEGER</code> and zero-scale <code>NUMERIC</code> types up to precision 38 to <code>INT64</code> type in
GoogleSQL for improved performance by default.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can set the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/search-index#column-granularity">column granularity</a> when you
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_search_index_statement">create a search index</a>,
which stores additional column information in your search index to further
optimize your search query performance. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_31_2026">March 31, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery <a href="/bigquery/docs/work-with-objectref"><code>ObjectRef</code> values</a>
now support the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>You can run <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/objectref_functions"><code>ObjectRef</code> functions</a>
with either
<a href="/bigquery/docs/work-with-objectref#authorizer_and_permissions">direct access or delegated access</a>.</li>
<li>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/objectref_functions#objmake_ref"><code>OBJ.MAKE_REF</code> function</a>
automatically fetches the latest Cloud Storage metadata and populates this in
the <code>ref.details</code> field.</li>
<li>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/objectref_functions#objget_read_url"><code>OBJ.GET_READ_URL</code> function</a>
returns a <code>STRUCT</code> value with a read URL and status columns and renders image
results in the Cloud console. Use this function when you don't require a
write URL.</li>
</ul>

<p>These features are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_30_2026">March 30, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The following forecasting and anomaly detection functions and updates are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA):</p>

<ul>
<li><p>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-detect-anomalies"><code>AI.DETECT_ANOMALIES</code> function</a>
supports providing a custom context window that determines how many of the
most recent data points should be used by the model.</p></li>
<li><p>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-forecast"><code>AI.FORECAST</code> function</a>
supports specifying the latest timestamp value for forecasting.</p></li>
<li>
<p>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-evaluate"><code>AI.EVALUATE</code> function</a>
supports the following:</p>

<ul>
<li><p>You can provide a custom context window that determines how many of the most
recent data points should be used by the model.</p></li>
<li><p>The function outputs the
<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mean_absolute_scaled_error">mean absolute scaled error</a>
for the time series.</p></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now create BigQuery <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/materialized-views-create#spanner">non-incremental materialized views over Spanner data</a>
to improve query performance by periodically caching results. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_26_2026">March 26, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use
<a href="/bigquery/docs/export-to-spanner#export_using_a_cloud_resource_connection">Cloud resource connections with <code>EXPORT DATA</code> statements</a>
to reverse ETL BigQuery data to Spanner. This
feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_25_2026">March 25, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>The <a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/gemini/docs/overview">Gemini for Google Cloud API</a>
(cloudaicompanion.googleapis.com) is now enabled for existing
BigQuery projects in the European jurisdiction.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/use-bigquery-migration-mcp">BigQuery Migration Service MCP server</a>
to perform SQL translation tasks, including translating SQL queries into
GoogleSQL syntax, generating DDL statements from SQL input queries, and getting
explanations of SQL translations.</p>

<p>This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>In BigQuery Data Transfer Service, you can
<a href="/bigquery/docs/hdfs-data-lake-transfer#monitor-transfer-status">monitor resource-level status reporting for Hive managed tables</a>
to track progress and view granular error details for individual tables.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration-assessment">BigQuery migration assessment for
Snowflake</a> to assess the complexity of
migrating from Snowflake to BigQuery. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_24_2026">March 24, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/datatransfer/mcp">BigQuery Data Transfer Service remote MCP
server</a> to enable AI agents to
create, manage, and run data transfers. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_23_2026">March 23, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The following functions are now
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA):</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-embed"><code>AI.EMBED</code></a>:
create embeddings from text or image data.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-similarity"><code>AI.SIMILARITY</code></a>:
compute the semantic similarity between pairs of text, pairs of images, or
across text and images.</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can clean, transform, and enrich data from files in Cloud Storage and Google
Drive in your BigQuery data preparations. For more information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions#open-data-prep-editor">Prepare data with Gemini</a>.
This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_19_2026">March 19, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use a <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-constraints">custom organization policy</a>
to allow or deny specific operations on routines. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_17_2026">March 17, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>In BigQuery ML, you can now
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#automatically_deployed_models">automatically deploy</a>
open models to Vertex AI endpoints. Automatically deployed models offer the
following benefits:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#managed-resources">Automatic Vertex AI resource management</a></li>
<li>Reserve open model resources by
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#reservation-affinity">using Compute Engine reservations</a>
</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#managed-model-undeployment">Automatic or immediate open model undeployment</a>
to save costs</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_16_2026">March 16, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery now lets you configure a <a href="/bigquery/docs/default-configuration#global-settings">global default location</a>.
This setting is used if the location isn't set or can't be inferred from the
request. You can set the default location at the organization or project level.</p>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_12_2026">March 12, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/advanced-runtime">BigQuery advanced runtime</a> is now enabled as
the default runtime for all projects.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_11_2026">March 11, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now  understand and debug BigQuery query performance with
a
<a href="/bigquery/docs/query-plan-explanation#query_text_heatmap">visual mapping of your SQL query in the query execution graph</a>.
A heatmap highlights the steps that consume more slot-time. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_09_2026">March 09, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>Updates to <a href="/bigquery/docs/conversational-analytics">conversational analytics</a> include the following improvements:</p>

<ul>
<li>ObjectRef support: BigQuery conversational analytics now
integrates with Google Cloud Storage through <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/objectref_functions">ObjectRef functions</a>.
This lets you reference and interact with unstructured data such as images and
PDFs in Cloud Storage buckets in your conversational analysis.</li>
<li>BQML support: BigQuery conversational analytics now supports <a href="/bigquery/docs/conversational-analytics#bigquery-ml-support">a set of BigQuery ML functions</a>,
including AI.FORECAST,  AI.DETECT_ANOMALIES, and AI.GENERATE. These functions
let you perform advanced analytics tasks with simple conversational prompts.</li>
<li>Chat with BigQuery results: You can now start conversations and chat with
query results in BigQuery Studio (SQL editor).</li>
<li>Enhanced support for partitioned tables: BigQuery conversational analytics can
now use BigQuery table partitioning. The agent can optimize SQL queries by
using partitioned columns such as date ranges on a date-partitioned table.
This can improve query performance and reduce costs.</li>
<li>Labels for agent-generated queries: BigQuery jobs initiated by the
conversational analytics agent are now labeled in <a href="/bigquery/docs/managing-jobs">BigQuery Job History</a>
in the Google Cloud Console. You can identify, filter, and analyze the jobs
run by the conversational analytics agent by referencing labels similar to
<code>{'ca-bq-job': 'true'}</code>. These labels can help with the following tasks:
<ul>
<li>Monitor and attribute cost.</li>
<li>Audit agent activity.</li>
<li>Analyze agent-generated query performance.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Suggest next questions (clickable): When working with BigQuery
conversational analytics, the agent now suggests questions that are directly
clickable in the Google Cloud console.</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is available in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_06_2026">March 06, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can create a <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-embedding-maas">remote model</a>
based on the Vertex AI <code>gemini-embedding-001</code> model, or a
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open">remote model</a>
based on an open embedding model from Vertex Model Garden or Hugging Face that
is deployed to Vertex AI.</p>

<p>You can then use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-embedding"><code>AI.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code> function</a>
with these remote models to generate embeddings. You can also use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-embed"><code>AI.EMBED</code> function</a>
directly with the <code>gemini-embedding-001</code> model endpoint.</p>

<p>These features are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/pipeline-connection-page">Pipelines &amp; Connections page</a>
to streamline your data integration tasks by using guided,
BigQuery-specific configuration workflows for services like
BigQuery Data Transfer Service, Datastream, and Pub/Sub.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_05_2026">March 05, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>An updated version of the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/odbc-jdbc-drivers#current_odbc_driver">Simba ODBC driver for BigQuery</a>
is now available.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use an alternate syntax when you call the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/search_functions#vector_search"><code>VECTOR_SEARCH</code> function</a>
to improve query performance when you search for a single vector. This feature
is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_04_2026">March 04, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Monitor dataset replication latency and network egress bytes in Cloud Monitoring
for BigQuery <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-replication#monitor-replication">cross-region replication</a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/managed-disaster-recovery#monitor-replication">managed disaster recovery</a>.
These metrics are <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/continuous-queries#spanner-example">continuous queries to stream BigQuery data to Spanner in real
time</a>. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_25_2026">February 25, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>Effective <em>June 1, 2026</em>, BigQuery will limit legacy SQL use. This depends on
whether your organization or project uses it from November 1, 2025, to June 1,
2026. If you don't use legacy SQL during this time, you won't be able to use it
after June 1, 2026. If you do use it, your existing workloads
will keep running, but new ones might not. For more information, see
<a href="https://docs.cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/legacy-sql-feature-availability">Legacy SQL feature availability</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_24_2026">February 24, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/create-data-agents#create-review-glossary-terms">create and review</a>
custom glossary terms in BigQuery for a conversational
analytics agent and you can review business glossary terms imported from
Dataplex Universal Catalog for an agent. These terms help an agent interpret your
prompts.</p>

<p>This feature is now in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_23_2026">February 23, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/restore-deleted-datasets">undelete a dataset</a> that
is within your time travel window to recover it to the state that it was in when
it was deleted. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_17_2026">February 17, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now run <a href="/bigquery/docs/global-queries">global queries</a>, which let you
reference data stored in more than one region in a single query. This feature is
in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>After March 17, 2026, when you enable BigQuery, the BigQuery MCP server is
automatically enabled.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-deprecated">Deprecated</span>
      <div><p>Control of MCP use with organization policies is deprecated. After
March 17, 2026, organization policies that use the
<code>gcp.managed.allowedMCPServices constraint</code> won't work, and you can control
MCP use with IAM deny policies. For more information about controlling MCP use,
see <a href="/mcp/control-mcp-use-iam">Control MCP use with IAM deny policies</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_12_2026">February 12, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-classify"><code>AI.CLASSIFY</code> function</a>
now supports classifying your input into multiple categories. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now provide descriptions for the fields in your custom output schema
when you use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate"><code>AI.GENERATE</code></a>
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-table"><code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code></a>
functions.
This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-dataset-insights">dataset insights</a>
to understand relationships between tables in a dataset by generating
relationship graphs and cross-table queries. You can automatically generate
dataset summaries, infer relationships across tables, and receive suggestions
for analytical questions. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_11_2026">February 11, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now run pipelines with three distinct execution methods: running all
tasks, running selected tasks, and running tasks with selected tags. For more
information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/create-pipelines#run-pipeline">Run a pipeline</a>.
This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_09_2026">February 09, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now customize the scope of data documentation scans for BigQuery tables
to generate specific insights. You can choose to generate only SQL queries,
only table and column descriptions, or all insights.</p>

<p>You can also create one-time data scans that execute immediately upon creation,
removing the need for a separate <code>run</code> command. These scans support a
Time to Live (TTL) setting to automatically delete the scan resource after
completion.</p>

<p>For more information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-table-insights#insights-bigquery-table">Generate insights for a BigQuery table</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_04_2026">February 04, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>Data transfers from the <a href="/bigquery/docs/youtube-channel-transfer">YouTube Channel</a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/youtube-content-owner-transfer">YouTube Content Owner</a>
data sources now support reach reports. For more information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/youtube-channel-transformation">YouTube Channel report transformation</a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/youtube-content-owner-transformation">YouTube Content Owner report transformation</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now associate <a href="/bigquery/docs/column-data-masking#data-policies-on-column">data policies directly on
columns</a>. This
feature enables direct database administration for controlling access and
applying masking and transformation rules at the column level. This feature is
now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="February_03_2026">February 03, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">

      <div><p>Gemini in BigQuery now processes data in the same jurisdiction (<code>US</code> or <code>EU</code>) as
your BigQuery datasets, or based upon user-specified location settings. For more
information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/gemini-locations">Where Gemini BigQuery processes your
data</a>.</p></div>

<h2 id="January_29_2026">January 29, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery now supports a <code>RANDOM_HASH</code> predefined masking rule. This rule returns
a hash of the column's value using a salted hash algorithm, and it provides
stronger security than the standard <code>Hash (SHA-256)</code> rule.</p>

<p>For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/column-data-masking-intro#masking_options">Data masking rules</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery now offers <a href="/bigquery/docs/conversational-analytics">conversational analytics</a>,
which accelerates data analysis by enabling insights through natural language.
Users can view a predefined sample agent, chat with their BigQuery data or
custom agents, and access those agents even outside of BigQuery. They can also
use <a href="/bigquery/docs/conversational-analytics#bigquery-ml-support">supported BigQuery ML functions</a>
in verified queries and in chat. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now create <a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/create-machine-learning-model-console">BigQuery ML models by using the
Google Cloud console</a>.</p>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="January_19_2026">January 19, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-breaking">Breaking</span>
      <div><p><a href="/dataform/docs/sql-workflows">Dataform workflows</a>,
<a href="/bigquery/docs/orchestrate-notebooks">BigQuery notebooks</a>,
<a href="/bigquery/docs/schedule-pipelines">pipelines</a>,
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/orchestrate-data-preparations">data preparations</a>
are enforcing strict act-as mode at the project level. To avoid failures and
maintain automatic releases, you must use custom service accounts instead of the
default Dataform service agent across all repositories. You must also grant the
Service Account User role (<code>roles/iam.serviceAccountUser</code>) to the default
Dataform service agent and relevant principals. For more information and to
verify act-as permissions, see
<a href="/dataform/docs/strict-act-as-mode">Use strict act-as mode</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_07_2026">January 07, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the Google-developed, open source
<a href="/bigquery/docs/jdbc-for-bigquery">Java Database Connectivity (JDBC) driver for BigQuery</a>
to connect your Java applications to BigQuery. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_06_2026">January 06, 2026</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_external_table_statement"><code>CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE</code></a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/load-statements"><code>LOAD DATA</code></a>
statements now support the following options:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<code>time_zone</code>: specify a time zone to use when loading data</li>
<li>
<code>date_format</code>, <code>datetime_format</code>, <code>time_format</code>, and <code>timestamp_format</code>: define how date and time values are formatted in your source files</li>
<li>
<code>null_markers</code>: define the strings that represent <code>NULL</code> values in CSV files.</li>
<li>
<code>source_column_match</code>: specify how loaded columns are matched to the schema. You can match columns by position or by name.</li>
</ul>

<p>These features are <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>

available</a> (GA).</p></div>

<h2 id="December_10_2025">December 10, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>

to enable LLM agents to perform a range of data-related tasks.</p>

<p>This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="December_02_2025">December 02, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>An updated version of the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/odbc-jdbc-drivers#current_odbc_driver">ODBC driver for BigQuery</a>
is now available.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now enable
<a href="/bigquery/docs/autonomous-embedding-generation">autonomous embedding generation</a>
on tables that you make with the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_table_statement"><code>CREATE TABLE</code> statement</a>.
When you do this, BigQuery maintains a column of embeddings on
the table based on a source column. When you add or modify data in the source
column, BigQuery automatically generates or updates the embedding
column for that data.</p>

<p>You can also use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-search"><code>AI.SEARCH</code></a>
function, enabling semantic search on tables that have autonomous embedding
generation enabled.</p>

<p>These features are in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>

available</a> (GA).</p></div>

<h2 id="November_20_2025">November 20, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the BigQuery Agent Analytics plugin within the Agent Development
Kit to export agent interaction data directly into BigQuery. This plugin
captures comprehensive logs of your agent's prompts, tool usage, and responses,
enabling you to analyze and visualize agent performance metrics. The plugin
leverages the BigQuery Storage Write API for efficient high-throughput
streaming. For more information on how to leverage this plugin in your agent,
see the
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/blog/products/data-analytics/introducing-bigquery-agent-analytics/?e=48754805">Announcing BigQuery Agent Analytics for the Google ADK</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

      <div><p>You can use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/json_functions#json_flatten"><code>JSON_FLATTEN</code> function</a>
to extract all non-array values that are either directly in the input <code>JSON</code>
value or children of one or more consecutively nested arrays in the input
<code>JSON</code> value. This function is available in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>

<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="November_18_2025">November 18, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use <a href="/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/models/gemini/3-pro">Gemini 3.0</a>
when you call generative AI functions in BigQuery,
such as <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate"><code>AI.GENERATE</code></a>.
You must use the full global endpoint argument:</p>

<p><code>https://aiplatform.googleapis.com/v1/projects/PROJECT_ID/locations/global/publishers/google/models/gemini-3-pro-preview</code>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Dataform now lets you automate the creation of
<a href="/dataform/docs/create-tables#create-iceberg-table">BigLake tables for Apache Iceberg in BigQuery</a>.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML now supports the following
<a href="/bigquery/docs/generative-ai-overview">generative AI functions</a>:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate"><code>AI.GENERATE</code></a>:
generate free text to accomplish a wide range of tasks, such as
translation, summarization, and classification, on any unstructured data,
including images, audio, video, and documents. It can also perform entity
extraction and generate structured output. This function is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-embed"><code>AI.EMBED</code></a>:
turn text, image, audio, video, or documents into embeddings. This function
is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-similarity"><code>AI.SIMILARITY</code></a>:
compute the semantic similarity between pairs of text, pairs of images, or
across text and images. This function is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</li>
<li>You can use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-bool"><code>AI.GENERATE_BOOL</code></a>,
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-double"><code>AI.GENERATE_DOUBLE</code></a>,
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-int"><code>AI.GENERATE_INT</code></a>
functions to generate scalar values, which are convenient for filtering,
scoring, and counting purposes.</li>
<li>Each of these functions supports
<a href="/bigquery/docs/permissions-for-ai-functions#run_generative_ai_queries_with_end-user_credentials">authentication with end-user credentials (EUC)</a>
to set up the necessary Vertex AI permissions.</li>
</ul>

<p>BigQuery ML now supports the following table-valued generative AI functions:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-table"><code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code></a>:
generate a table of structured output from unstructured data including
text, images, audio, and video.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-text"><code>AI.GENERATE_TEXT</code></a>
is the new, preferred version of <code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code>, which has the same
functionality but with simplified column output names.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-embedding"><code>AI.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code></a>
is the new, preferred version of <code>ML.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code>, which has the same
functionality but with simplified column output names.</li>
<li>These functions are all
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-insights#modes">publish data insights</a>,
including query recommendations and
auto-generated table and column descriptions, to the Dataplex Universal Catalog.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="November_11_2025">November 11, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The BigQuery <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#open-overview">Overview page</a>
is now your hub for discovering tutorials, features, and resources to help you
get the most out of BigQuery. It provides guided paths for users
of all skill levels. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/interactive-sql-translator">interactive SQL translator</a>, the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/api-sql-translator">translation API</a>, and the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/batch-sql-translator">batch SQL translator</a> to translate the
following SQL dialects into GoogleSQL:</p>

<ul>
<li>Apache Impala SQL</li>
<li>GoogleSQL (BigQuery)</li>
</ul>

<p>Impala SQL translation can be used to migrate Cloudera and Apache Hadoop SQL
workloads that use Impala as a query engine.</p>

<p>GoogleSQL (BigQuery) translation can be used to verify and iteratively customize
your translated SQL queries after an initial translation from an external
dialect. For example, you can apply systematic query rewrites using <a href="/bigquery/docs/config-yaml-translation#optimize_and_improve_the_performance_of_translated_sql">YAML
configurations</a>
to customize and optimize your GoogleSQL queries before deploying it.</p>

<p>These features are in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-constraints">custom constraints</a> with an
Organization Policy to provide more granular control over specific fields for
BigQuery dataset resources. This feature is <a href="/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="November_10_2025">November 10, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions#aggregate">aggregate</a>
and <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions#deduplicate">deduplicate</a>
table data with Gemini assistance in your
<a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-introduction">BigQuery data preparations</a>.
These features are <a href="/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Partitioning is now available for
<a href="/bigquery/docs/iceberg-tables#use_partitioning">BigLake tables for Apache Iceberg in BigQuery</a>.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery ML now supports the <code>TimesFM 2.5</code>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/timesfm-model">time series foundational model</a>.
You can use the <code>TimesFM 2.5</code> model in the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-forecast"><code>AI.FORECAST</code></a>,
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-evaluate"><code>AI.EVALUATE</code></a>,
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-detect-anomalies"><code>AI.DETECT_ANOMALIES</code></a>
functions to achieve better forecasting accuracy and lower latency.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery ML now offers the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-detect-anomalies"><code>AI.DETECT_ANOMALIES</code> function</a>.
Use the <code>AI.DETECT_ANOMALIES</code> function with a TimesFM model to
<a href="/bigquery/docs/anomaly-detection-overview">detect anomalies</a>
in time series data, using historical data as a baseline.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="November_06_2025">November 06, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>The research paper <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2510.24452">ARIMA_PLUS: Large-scale, Accurate, Automatic and
Interpretable In-Database Time Series Forecasting and Anomaly Detection in
Google BigQuery</a> is now publicly available.
This paper describes the algorithms behind the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-time-series"><code>ARIMA_PLUS</code></a>
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-multivariate-time-series"><code>ARIMA_PLUS_XREG</code></a>
models for time series forecasting and anomaly detection, and demonstrates the
high performance, scalability, explainability, and customizability of the
models.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="November_05_2025">November 05, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/query-syntax#match_recognize_clause"><code>MATCH_RECOGNIZE</code> clause</a>
in your SQL queries to filter and aggregate matches across rows in a table.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/google-ads-transfer">BigQuery Data Transfer Service for Google Ads</a> now supports <a href="https://developers.google.com/google-ads/api/fields/v21/overview">Google Ads API v21</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now
<a href="/bigquery/docs/data-insights#generate-column-table-descriptions">generate table and column descriptions</a>
in all supported Gemini languages when you generate data insights.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now generate <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-insights#rest">data insights</a> when you
create a
<a href="/dataplex/docs/reference/rest/v1/projects.locations.dataScans"><code>DataScan</code></a>
using the Dataplex API. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="November_04_2025">November 04, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration-custom-org-policies">custom organization policies with the BigQuery migration
service</a> to allow or deny specific
operations during a BigQuery migration to meet your organization's compliance
and security requirements. This includes an option to disable AI suggestions
during a migration. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="October_31_2025">October 31, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>We have <a href="https://workspaceupdates.googleblog.com/2025/10/powerful-pivot-tables-connected-sheets.html">increased the row capacity</a>
for pivot tables backed by BigQuery in <a href="/bigquery/docs/connected-sheets">Connected Sheets</a>
from 100,000 to 200,000 rows.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_30_2025">October 30, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The
<a href="/biglake/docs/blms-rest-catalog">Apache Iceberg REST catalog in BigLake metastore</a>
is now
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA) with several new features, including BigQuery catalog federation,
credential vending, and catalog management in the Google Cloud console.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_29_2025">October 29, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-tasks#prioritize_idle_slots_with_reservation_groups">group
reservations</a>
together to prioritize idle slot sharing within the group. Reservations within a
reservation group share idle slots with each other before making them available
to other reservations in the project, giving you more control over slot
allocation for high-priority workloads. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_28_2025">October 28, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The BigQuery Data Transfer Service can now transfer data from the
following data sources:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/facebook-ads-transfer">Facebook Ads</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/salesforce-transfer">Salesforce</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/sfmc-transfer">Salesforce Marketing Cloud</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/servicenow-transfer">ServiceNow</a></li>
</ul>

<p>Transfers from these data sources are now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Subscriber email logging lets you log the principal identifiers of users
who execute jobs and queries against linked datasets. You can enable
logging at the
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/analytics-hub-manage-listings#create_a_listing">listing level</a>
and the
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/analytics-hub-manage-exchanges#create-exchange">data exchange level</a>.
The logged data is available in the <code>job_principal_subject</code> field of the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/information-schema-shared-dataset-usage"><code>INFORMATION_SCHEMA.SHARED_DATASET_USAGE</code> view</a>.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_27_2025">October 27, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The administrative jobs explorer now includes a <a href="/bigquery/docs/admin-jobs-explorer#get-job-details">job details
page</a> to help you diagnose
and troubleshoot queries. The <strong>Performance</strong> tab compiles query information
including the execution graph, SQL text, execution history, performance
variance, and system load during execution. You can also <a href="/bigquery/docs/admin-jobs-explorer#compare-jobs">compare two
jobs</a> to identify discrepancies
and potential areas to improve query performance.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery now offers the following
<a href="/bigquery/docs/generative-ai-overview#managed_ai_functions">managed AI functions</a>
that use Gemini to help you filter, join, rank, and classify your data:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-if"><code>AI.IF</code></a>:
Filter and join text or multimodal data based on a condition described in natural language.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-score"><code>AI.SCORE</code></a>:
Rate text or multimodal input to rank your data by quality, similarity, or other criteria.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-classify"><code>AI.CLASSIFY</code></a>:
Classify text into user-defined categories.</li>
</ul>

<p>These functions are in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-engineering-agent-pipelines">use the Data Engineering Agent</a>
to use Gemini in BigQuery to build and modify data
pipelines to ingest data into BigQuery. This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the Apache Arrow format to
<a href="/bigquery/docs/write-api#arrow-handling">stream data to BigQuery with the Storage Write API</a>.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>

<h2 id="October_23_2025">October 23, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery is now offering
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">early access</a>
to conversational analytics. Conversational analytics accelerates data analysis
by enabling quick insights through natural language. Users can chat with their
BigQuery data, create custom agents, and access those agents even outside of
BigQuery. To enroll in conversational analytics early access, fill out the
<a href="https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSe5KhRr81uUce6mKj8YrV1iFezGIydTxOcx8wUTqcBJP3e7vg/viewform">request form</a>.</p></div>

<h2 id="October_22_2025">October 22, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-issue">Issue</span>
      <div><p>Support for
<a href="/bigquery/docs/table-functions#table_parameters">table parameters in table-value functions (TVFs)</a>
has been temporarily disabled. We are working to restore this feature as soon
as possible.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use custom constraints with Organization Policy to provide more
granular control over specific fields for some BigQuery sharing
resources. For more information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/analytics-hub-custom-constraints">Manage Sharing data exchanges and listings using custom constraints</a>.
This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML now offers a built-in
<a href="/bigquery/docs/timesfm-model">TimesFM univariate time series forecasting model</a>
that implements Google Research's open source TimesFM model. You can use
BigQuery ML's built-in TimesFM model with the following functions:</p>

<ul>
<li>Use
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-forecast"><code>AI.FORECAST</code></a>
to perform forecasting. This function now supports a larger context window.</li>
<li>Use
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-evaluate"><code>AI.EVALUATE</code></a>
to evaluate forecasted data against a reference time series based on
historical data.</li>
</ul>

<p>To try using a TimesFM model with the <code>AI.FORECAST</code> function, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/timesfm-time-series-forecasting-tutorial">Forecast a time series with a TimesFM univariate model</a>.</p>

<p>This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="October_20_2025">October 20, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>In BigQuery ML, you can now fully manage open models as Vertex AI endpoints.
BigQuery-managed open models offer the following benefits:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#managed-resources">Manage Vertex AI resource by using SQL queries</a></li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#managed-model-undeployment">Automatic or immediate open model undeployment</a>
to save costs</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#machine-type">Customize model deployment machine types</a>
or reserve open model resources by
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open#reservation-affinity">using Compute Engine reservations</a>
</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/create-notebooks#cells">visualization cells</a> to
automatically
<a href="/bigquery/docs/visualize-data-colab">generate a visualization</a>
of any DataFrame in your notebook.
You can customize the columns, chart type, aggregations, colors , labels, and
title.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_16_2025">October 16, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now access repositories by clicking Repositories in the Explorer pane.
A new tab opens that displays a list of repositories. The Explorer pane no
longer has a bottom pane for repositories. When you open a workspace in a
repository, it opens in the Git repository pane in the left pane. These
features are available in BigQuery Studio in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The following features are now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA) in BigQuery Studio:</p>

<ul>
<li><p>To streamline resource discovery and access, the <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#explorer_panel">left Explorer
pane</a> has been reorganized
into three sections: Explorer, Classic Explorer, and Git repository. You can
still use the Classic Explorer, which provides the complete resources tree.</p></li>
<li><p>In the Explorer pane, you can use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#explorer_pane">search
feature</a> to find BigQuery
resources in your organization. The results appear in a new tab in the
details pane. You can use filters to narrow your search.</p></li>
<li><p>You can access job histories by clicking <a href="/bigquery/docs/managing-jobs">Job
history</a> in the Explorer pane. A new tab opens
that displays a list of job histories. BigQuery Studio no longer has a
bottom pane for job history.</p></li>
<li><p>To reduce tab proliferation, clicking a resource opens it within the same
tab. To open the resource in a separate tab, press <kbd>Ctrl</kbd> (or
<kbd>Command</kbd> on macOS) and click the resource. To prevent the current
tab from getting its content replaced, double-click the tab. The name
changes from italicized to regular font. If you still
lose your resource, you can click <span class="material-symbols-outlined">tab_recent</span> Recent tabs in the
details pane to find the resource.</p></li>
<li><p>You can use breadcrumbs to navigate through different tabs and
resources in the details pane.</p></li>
<li><p>In the Home tab, the <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#welcome_tab">What's new section</a>
contains a list of new capabilities and changes to the BigQuery Studio.</p></li>
<li><p>The notebook action bar is consolidated by default to give you more screen
space for writing code.</p></li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="October_09_2025">October 09, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>An updated version of the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/odbc-jdbc-drivers#odbc_release_3151022">ODBC driver for BigQuery</a> is now available.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can set a <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management#predictable">maximum slot
limit</a> for a
reservation. You can configure the maximum reservation size when creating or
updating a reservation. This feature is now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can <a href="/bigquery/docs/slots#fairness">allocate idle slots fairly</a> across
reservations within a single admin project. This ensures each reservation
receives an approximately equal share of available capacity. This feature is now
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p><a href="/gemini/docs/bigquery/security-privacy-compliance">Security, privacy, and compliance for Gemini in
BigQuery</a> details how
customer data is protected and processed by Gemini in BigQuery.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_08_2025">October 08, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-breaking">Breaking</span>
      <div><p>The <a href="/bigquery/quotas#query_jobs">default limit of <code>QueryUsagePerDay</code></a> for
on-demand pricing has changed. The default limit of all new projects is now 200
TiB. For existing projects, the default limit has been set based on your
project's usage over the last 30 days. Projects that have <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-quotas">custom cost
controls</a> configured or that use
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management">reservations</a> aren't affected.
If the new limit might affect your workload, create a <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-quotas">custom cost
control</a> based on your workload needs.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management#flexible">specify which reservation a query uses at
runtime</a>, and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management#securable">set IAM
policies directly on
reservations</a>. This
provides more flexibility and fine-grained control over resource management.
This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can set <a href="/bigquery/docs/labels-intro">labels</a> on reservations. These labels
can be used to organize your reservations and for billing analysis. This feature
is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_07_2025">October 07, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>As of February 25, 2025, enhancements to the <a href="/bigquery/docs/slots-autoscaling-intro">workload management
autoscaler</a> that were announced on <a href="/bigquery/docs/release-notes#July_31_2024">July
31, 2024</a> have rolled out to all users.
These enhancements are <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="October_06_2025">October 06, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/information-schema-shared-dataset-usage#schema"><code>INFORMATION_SCHEMA.SHARED_DATASET_USAGE</code> view</a>
now includes the following schema fields to support usage metrics for
external tables and routines:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<code>shared_resource_id</code>: the ID of the queried resource</li>
<li>
<code>shared_resource_type</code>: the type of the queried resource</li>
<li>
<code>referenced_tables</code>: Contains <code>project_id</code>,
<code>dataset_id</code>, <code>table_id</code>, and <code>processed_bytes</code>
fields of the base table.</li>
</ul>

<p>These fields are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now set the priority of BigQuery jobs initiated by
Dataform workflows to run queries as interactive jobs that start
running as quickly as possible or as batch jobs with lower priority. For more
information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/schedule-pipelines#create-schedule">Create a pipeline schedule</a>
and
<a href="/dataform/reference/rest/v1/InvocationConfig">InvocationConfig</a>.
This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The BigQuery Data Transfer Service can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/google-analytics-4-transfer">transfer reporting data from Google Analytics 4</a>
into BigQuery. You can also include custom reports from
Google Analytics 4 in your data transfer. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The BigQuery Data Transfer Service can now transfer data from the
following data sources:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/paypal-transfer">PayPal</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/stripe-transfer">Stripe</a></li>
</ul>

<p>Transfers from these data sources are supported in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>

<h5 id="features">Features</h5>

<ul>
<li>
<strong>bigquery/analyticshub:</strong> You can now configure listings for multiple regions for shared datasets and linked dataset replicas in BigQuery sharing (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/commit/10e67efccf048adea11d3ecba8d0c625455e545f">10e67ef</a>)</li>
<li>
<strong>bigquery/reservation:</strong> Add a new field <code>failover_mode</code> to <code>.google.cloud.bigquery.reservation.v1.FailoverReservationRequest</code> that allows users to choose between the HARD or SOFT failover modes when they initiate a failover operation on a reservation (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/commit/10e67efccf048adea11d3ecba8d0c625455e545f">10e67ef</a>)</li>
<li>
<strong>bigquery/reservation:</strong> Add a new field <code>soft_failover_start_time</code> in the existing <code>replication_status</code> in <code>.google.cloud.bigquery.reservation.v1.Reservation</code> to provide visibility into the state of ongoing soft failover operations on the reservation (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/commit/10e67efccf048adea11d3ecba8d0c625455e545f">10e67ef</a>)</li>
<li>
<strong>bigquery:</strong> Add support for MaxSlots (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/issues/12958">#12958</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/google-cloud-go/commit/a3c0aca6edb873132360b46c7bb1a2aaab6d3fce">a3c0aca</a>)</li>

<h2 id="September_29_2025">September 29, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>To simplify access management for your Iceberg tables, you
can use <a href="/bigquery/docs/blms-rest-catalog">credential vending mode with the Apache Iceberg REST catalog</a> in BigLake metastore. Credential vending removes
the need for catalog users to have direct access to Cloud Storage buckets. This
feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now create BigQuery
<a href="/bigquery/docs/materialized-views-create#spanner">non-incremental materialized views over Spanner data</a>
to improve query performance by periodically caching results.
This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery data preparation supports unnesting arrays, which expands each
array element into its own row for easier analysis. For more information, see
<a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions#unnest-arrays">Unnest arrays</a>.
This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally
available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/history-based-optimizations">History-based query optimizations</a>
are now enabled by default. If history-based optimizations have been previously
disabled, you can <a href="/bigquery/docs/history-based-optimizations#enable-history-based-optimization">re-enable history-based optimizations</a>
for your project or organization.</p></div>
    </div>

    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">

canvas</a> now
supports destination table nodes. Destination table nodes let you persist query

available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="September_24_2025">September 24, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery ML now supports
<a href="/bigquery/docs/model-monitoring-overview#monitoring_visualization">visualization of model monitoring metrics</a>.
This feature lets you use charts and graphs to
<a href="/vertex-ai/docs/model-monitoring/run-monitoring-job#analyze_monitoring_job_results">analyze model monitoring function output</a>.
You can use metric visualization with the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-validate-data-skew"><code>ML.VALIDATE_DATA_SKEW</code></a>
and
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-validate-data-drift"><code>ML.VALIDATE_DATA_DRIFT</code></a>
functions. This feature is
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>For command-line users, BigQuery is now integrated with the Gemini CLI to provide an agentic CLI experience. Using the dedicated <a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/develop-with-gemini-cli">Gemini CLI extensions for BigQuery</a>, you can search, explore, analyze, and gain insights from your data by asking natural language questions, generating forecasts, and running contribution analysis directly from the command line. This feature is available in beta.</p></div>
    </div>

You can then use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-embedding"><code>ML.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code> function</a> with this remote model to generate embeddings. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>

For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/create-pipelines">Create pipelines</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now create a <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open">remote model based on an open embedding model from Vertex Model Garden or Hugging Face that is deployed to Vertex AI</a>. Options include E5 Embedding and other leading open embedding generation models. You can then use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-embedding"><code>ML.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code> function</a> with this remote model to generate embeddings.</p>

<p>Try this feature with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-text-embedding-tutorial-open-models">Generate text embeddings by using an open model and the <code>ML.GENERATE_EMBEDDING</code> function</a> tutorial.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
