<h2 id="August_21_2025">August 21, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div>
<p>Starting September 25, 2025, the BigQuery Data Transfer Service for third-party SAAS and database connectors will update to a consumption-based pricing model. With this new pricing model, you will be charged based on the compute resources consumed by your data transfers, measured in slot-hours. For more information, see <a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/pricing#section-5">Data Transfer Service pricing</a>. This pricing update applies to the following third-party connectors when they are <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available (GA)</a>:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/facebook-ads-transfer">Facebook Ads</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/mysql-transfer">MySQL</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/oracle-transfer">Oracle</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/postgresql-transfer">PostgreSQL</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/salesforce-transfer">Salesforce</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/sfmc-transfer">Salesforce Marketing Cloud</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/servicenow-transfer">ServiceNow</a></li>
<li>Other third-party connectors planned for future releases</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="July_31_2025">July 31, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can manage data profile scans and data quality scans across your project by using the <strong>Metadata curation</strong> page in the Google Cloud console. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-profile-scan">Profile your data</a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-quality-scan">Scan for data quality issues</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery ML now can automatically detect model quota increases in Vertex AI, and automatically adjusts the quota for any BigQuery ML functions that use those models. You no longer need to email the BigQuery ML team to increase model quota.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML has improved throughput by more than 100x for the following
generative AI functions:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-text"><code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-table"><code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate"><code>AI.GENERATE</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-bool"><code>AI.GENERATE_BOOL</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-double"><code>AI.GENERATE_DOUBLE</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-int"><code>AI.GENERATE_INT</code></a></li>
</ul>

<p>Actual performance varies based on the number of input and output tokens in the
request, but a typical 6-hour job can now process millions of rows. For more
information, see
<a href="/bigquery/quotas#generative_ai_functions">Generative AI functions</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/continuous-queries-introduction">continuous queries</a> to <a href="/bigquery/docs/export-to-spanner">export BigQuery data to Spanner in real time</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="July_30_2025">July 30, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>The Gemini for Google Cloud API (cloudaicompanion.googleapis.com) is now enabled by default for most BigQuery projects. Exceptions include projects where customers have opted out, and those linked to accounts based in EMEA regions including <a href="/bigquery/docs/locations#supported_locations">BigQuery Europe, Middle East, and Africa regions</a>.</p></div>

<h2 id="July_22_2025">July 22, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/query-syntax#match_recognize_clause"><code>MATCH_RECOGNIZE</code> clause</a> in your SQL queries to filter and aggregate matches across rows in a table. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_external_table_statement"><code>CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE</code></a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/load-statements"><code>LOAD DATA</code></a> statements now support the following options in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<code>null_markers</code>: define the strings that represent <code>NULL</code> values in CSV files.</li>
<li>
<code>source_column_match</code>: specify how loaded columns are matched to the schema. You can match columns by position or by name.</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="/assured-workloads/access-transparency/docs/supported-services">Access Transparency</a> supports <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-introduction">BigQuery data preparation</a> in the <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">GA</a> stage.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/vectorindex_functions#vector_indexstatistics"><code>VECTOR_INDEX.STATISTICS</code> function</a> to calculate how much an indexed table's data has drifted between when a
vector index was created and the present. If table data has changed enough
to require a <a href="/bigquery/docs/vector-index#rebuild_a_vector_index">vector index rebuild</a>, you can use the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#alter_vector_index_rebuild_statement"><code>ALTER VECTOR INDEX REBUILD</code> statement</a>
to rebuild the vector index. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="July_17_2025">July 17, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/pipe-syntax#with_pipe_operator"><code>WITH</code> pipe operator</a> to define common table expressions in your pipe syntax queries. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/pipe-syntax#select_pipe_operator">named windows</a> in your pipe syntax queries. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>

Google Cloud console user interface</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>

You can also reply to existing comments or get a link to them. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>

<h2 id="July_08_2025">July 08, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>Starting August 1, 2025, GoogleSQL will become the default dialect for queries run from the command line interface (CLI) or API. To use LegacySQL, you will need to explicitly specify it in your requests or <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#alter_project_set_options_statement">set the configuration setting</a> <code>default_sql_dialect_option</code> to <code>'default_legacy_sql'</code> at the project or organization level.</p></div>
    </div>

    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>

<a href="/bigquery/docs/orchestrate-data-preparations#run-undeployed-manually">Manually run a data preparation in development</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="June_26_2025">June 26, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/search-intro">BigQuery search indexes</a> provide free index management until your organization reaches the <a href="/bigquery/quotas#index_limits">limit</a> in a given region. You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/information-schema-indexes-by-organization"><code>INFORMATION_SCHEMA.SEARCH_INDEXES_BY_ORGANIZATION</code> view</a> to understand your current consumption towards that limit, broken down by projects and tables. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the
use the <code>PARTITION BY</code> clause of the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_vector_index_statement"><code>CREATE VECTOR INDEX</code> statement</a> to <a href="/bigquery/docs/vector-index#partitions">partition TreeAH vector indexes</a>. Partitioning enables partition pruning and can decrease I/O costs. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="June_18_2025">June 18, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-quality-scan">publish the results of a data quality scan as Dataplex Universal Catalog metadata</a>. Previously, data quality scan results were published only to the Google Cloud console. The latest results are saved to the entry that represents the source table. You can view the results in the Google Cloud console. If you want to enable catalog publishing for an existing data quality scan, you must edit the scan and re-enable the publishing option. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>

<h2 id="June_16_2025">June 16, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">

    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/merchant-center-best-sellers-schema">Merchant Center best sellers report</a> supports multi-client accounts (MCAs). If you have an MCA, you can use the <code>aggregator_id</code> to query the tables. The <code>BestSellersEntityProductMapping</code> table maps the best-selling entities to the products in the sub-accounts' inventory. This provides a consolidated view of best-selling products, which you can then join with product data for more detailed insights. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>In BigQuery ML, you can now forecast multiple time series at once by using the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-multivariate-time-series#time_series_id_col"><code>TIME_SERIES_ID_COL</code> option</a> that is available in <code>ARIMA_PLUS_XREG</code> multivariate time series models. Try this feature with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/arima-plus-xreg-multiple-time-series-forecasting-tutorial">Forecast multiple time series with a multivariate model</a> tutorial. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery now offers the following Gemini-enhanced SQL translation features:</p>

<ul>
<li>Create <a href="/bigquery/docs/config-yaml-translation#ai_yaml_guidelines">Gemini-based configuration YAML files</a> to generate AI suggestions for batch or interactive SQL translations. This feature is now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</li>
<li>After making a batch SQL translation, review your translation output, including Gemini-based suggestions, using the <a href="/bigquery/docs/batch-sql-translator#code-tab">code tab</a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/batch-sql-translator#configuration_tab">configuration tab</a>. This feature is now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</li>
<li>When making an interactive SQL translation, <a href="/bigquery/docs/interactive-sql-translator#create-apply-rules">create and apply Gemini-enhanced translation rules</a> to customize your SQL inputs. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</li>
</ul>
</div>

<p>The following GoogleSQL functions are now available in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>:</p>

<ul>
<li>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/array_functions#array_first"><code>ARRAY_FIRST</code> function</a> returns the first element of the input array.</li>
<li>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/array_functions#array_last"><code>ARRAY_LAST</code> function</a> returns the last element of the input array.</li>
<li>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/array_functions#array_slice"><code>ARRAY_SLICE</code> function</a> returns an array that contains consecutive elements from the input array.</li>
</ul>

      <div>
<p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-definition-language#create_external_table_statement"><code>CREATE EXTERNAL TABLE</code></a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/load-statements"><code>LOAD DATA</code></a> statements now support the following options in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<code>time_zone</code>: specify a time zone to use when loading data</li>
<li>
<code>date_format</code>, <code>datetime_format</code>, <code>time_format</code>, and <code>timestamp_format</code>: define how date and time values are formatted in your source files</li>

This is achieved by showing or hiding user interface elements. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>

This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>

For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/dataframes-dbt">Use BigQuery DataFrames in dbt</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>

For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/schedule-pipelines#create-schedule">Create a pipeline schedule</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>

      <div><p>You can now create <a href="/bigquery/docs/event-driven-transfer">event-driven transfers</a> when transferring data from Cloud Storage to BigQuery. Event-driven transfers can automatically trigger transfer runs when data in your Cloud Storage bucket has been modified or added. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>

<h2 id="May_27_2025">May 27, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery offers <a href="/bigquery/docs/running-queries#optional-job-creation">optional job creation mode</a> to speed up small queries that you use in your dashboards, data exploration, and other workflows. This mode automatically optimizes eligible queries and uses a cache to improve latency. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>

<h2 id="May_22_2025">May 22, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>Starting March 17 2026, the <code>bigquery.datasets.getIamPolicy</code>
IAM permission is required to view a dataset's access controls and to query the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/information-schema-object-privileges"><code>INFORMATION_SCHEMA.OBJECT_PRIVILEGES</code></a>
view. The <code>bigquery.datasets.setIamPolicy</code> permission is required to update a
dataset's access controls or to <a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/dataset-access-control#changes_to_api_methods">create a dataset with access controls using the
API</a>. For more information on this change and how to opt into early enforcement, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/dataset-access-control">Changes to dataset-level access controls</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>When you migrate Teradata data to BigQuery using the BigQuery Data Transfer Service, you can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration/teradata-overview#using_translation_engine_output_for_schema">specify the outputs of the BigQuery translation engine to use as schema mapping</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can use <a href="/bigquery/docs/custom-constraints">custom constraints</a> with Organization Policy to provide more granular control over specific fields for some BigQuery resources. This feature is available in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>When you <a href="/gemini/docs/bigquery/set-up-gemini">Set up Gemini in BigQuery</a> you are now prompted to grant the BigQuery Studio User and BigQuery Studio Admin roles. These roles now include permission to use Gemini in BigQuery features. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can select multiple columns and perform data preparation tasks on them, including dropping columns. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions">Prepare data with Gemini</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="May_21_2025">May 21, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>You can now perform <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model#supervised_tuning">supervised tuning</a> on a BigQuery ML <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model">remote model</a> based on a Vertex AI <code>gemini-2.0-flash-001</code> or <code>gemini-2.0-flash-lite-001</code> model.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">

<section><h3 id="python_7">Python</h3>
<h4 id="3320_2025-05-12_-_yanked">
<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/compare/v3.31.0...v3.32.0">3.32.0</a> (2025-05-12)  - YANKED</h4>

<h4 id="reason_this_release_was_yanked">Reason this release was yanked:</h4>

<p>PR #2154 caused a performance regression.</p>

<h5 id="features_2">Features</h5>

<ul>
<li>Add dataset access policy version attribute (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2169">#2169</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/b7656b97c1bd6c204d0508b1851d114719686655">b7656b9</a>)</li>

<h5 id="bug_fixes_4">Bug Fixes</h5>

<ul>
<li>
<code>query()</code> now warns when <code>job_id</code> is set and the default <code>job_retry</code> is ignored (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2167">#2167</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/ca1798aaee2d5905fe688d3097f8ee5c989da333">ca1798a</a>)</li>

</ul></section>
</div></devsite-selector></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p><a href="/bigquery/docs/continuous-queries-introduction">Continuous queries</a> let you build long-lived, continuously processing SQL statements that can analyze, process, and perform machine learning (ML) inference on incoming data in BigQuery in real time.</p>

<ul>
<li>To monitor your continuous queries, you can use a <a href="/bigquery/docs/continuous-queries#custom-job-id">custom job ID prefix</a> to simplify filtering or view <a href="/bigquery/docs/monitoring-dashboard#metrics">metrics specific to continuous queries</a> in Cloud Monitoring.</li>
<li>Continuous queries can use <a href="/bigquery/docs/continuous-queries-introduction#slots_autoscaling">slot autoscaling</a> to dynamically scale allocated capacity to accommodate your workload.</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Spanner now supports <a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/spanner-federated-queries#cross_region_queries">cross regional federated queries</a> from BigQuery which allow BigQuery users to query Spanner tables from regions other than their BigQuery region. Users don't incur <a href="/spanner/pricing#network">Spanner network egress charges</a> during the preview period. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="May_14_2025">May 14, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration/snowflake-transfer">schedule automated data transfers from Snowflake to BigQuery</a> using the BigQuery Data Transfer Service. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Vector indexes support the <a href="/bigquery/docs/vector-index#tree-ah-index">TreeAH index type</a>, which uses Google's ScaNN algorithm. The TreeAH index is optimized for efficient batch processing, capable of handling anywhere from a few thousand to hundreds of thousands of embeddings at once. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery now supports cross-region transfers for <a href="/bigquery/docs/batch-loading-data">batch loading</a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/exporting-data#export-data-in-bigquery">exporting</a> data. You can load or export your data from any region or multi-region to any other region or multi-region using a single <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/bq-cli-reference#bq_load"><code>bq load</code></a>, <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/load-statements#load_data_statement"><code>LOAD DATA</code></a>, <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/bq-cli-reference#bq_extract"><code>bq extract</code></a>, or <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/export-statements#export_data_statement"><code>EXPORT DATA</code></a> statement. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="May_13_2025">May 13, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The following SQL features are now <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA) in BigQuery:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-types#group_with_structs"><code>GROUP BY STRUCT</code></a> and the <code>SELECT DISTINCT</code> clause.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/data-types#group_with_arrays"><code>GROUP BY ARRAY</code></a>  and the <code>SELECT DISTINCT</code> clause.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/query-syntax#group_by_all"><code>GROUP BY ALL</code></a> clause.</li>
</ul>
</div>

      <div>
<p><a href="/bigquery/docs/admin-resource-charts#view-resource-utilization">BigQuery resource utilization charts</a> have the following changes:</p>

<ul>
<li>The default timeline shown in the event timeline chart has changed from one to six hours.</li>
<li>Several improvements have been made to the views, including a new reservation slot usage view. This view helps monitor idle, baseline, and autoscaled slot usage.</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>

    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use BigQuery and BigQuery DataFrames to enable multimodal analysis, transformation, and data engineering (ELT) workflows in both SQL and Python. Use multimodal data features to do the following:</p>

<ul>
<li><p>Integrate unstructured data into standard tables by using  <a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#objectref_values"><code>ObjectRef</code></a> values, and then work with this data in analysis and transformation workflows by using <a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#objectrefruntime_values"><code>ObjectRefRuntime</code></a> values.</p></li>
<li><p>Use generative AI to analyze multimodal data and generate embeddings by using
<a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#generative_ai_functions">BigQuery ML SQL functions</a> or <a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#generative_ai_methods">BigQuery DataFrames methods</a>
with Gemini and multimodal embedding models.</p></li>
<li><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#multimodal_dataframes">Create multimodal DataFrames</a> in BigQuery DataFrames, and then use <a href="/bigquery/docs/analyze-multimodal-data#object_transformation_methods">object transformation methods</a> to transform images and chunk PDF files.</p></li>
<li><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/multimodal-data-sql-tutorial">Use Python user-defined functions (UDFs)</a> to transform images and chunk PDF files.</p></li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>

<h2 id="April_23_2025">April 23, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management#flexible">specify which reservation a query uses at runtime</a>, and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reservations-workload-management#securable">set IAM policies directly on reservations</a>. This provides more flexibility and fine-grained control over resource management. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">public preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">

You can configure the maximum reservation size when creating or updating a reservation. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">public preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/slots#fairness">allocate idle slots fairly</a> across reservations within a single admin project. This ensures each reservation receives an approximately equal share of available capacity. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">public preview</a>.</p></div>

<h4 id="794_2025-04-02">

    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery now provides spend-based <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-cud">committed use discounts</a> (CUDs). Spend-based committed use discounts provide a discount in exchange for your commitment to spend a minimum amount per hour on PAYG compute resources <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-cud#usage">listed here</a>. You can purchase CUDs with a one or three year commitment period.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>

    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div>
<p>You can get the required permissions to use BigQuery data preparation through the <a href="/iam/docs/roles-permissions/bigquery#bigquery.studioUser">BigQuery Studio User</a> (<code>roles/bigquery.studioUser</code>) and <a href="/iam/docs/roles-permissions/cloudaicompanion#cloudaicompanion.user">Gemini for Google Cloud User</a> (<code>roles/cloudaicompanion.user</code>) roles, and permission to access the data you're preparing.</p>

<p>BigQuery data preparation no longer requires that you have the permissions granted by the following IAM roles:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/iam/docs/roles-permissions/bigquery#bigquery.dataEditor">BigQuery Data Editor </a>(<code>roles/bigquery.dataEditor</code>)</li>
<li>
<a href="/iam/docs/roles-permissions/serviceusage#serviceusage.serviceUsageConsumer">Service Usage Consumer</a> (<code>roles/serviceusage.serviceUsageConsumer</code>)</li>
</ul>

<p>For more information about the required roles, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/manage-data-preparations">Manage data preparations</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="April_09_2025">April 09, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p><em>Dataplex Catalog</em> has been renamed <em>BigQuery universal catalog</em>. You'll see this new name in the product page of the Google Cloud console, the documentation set, and the marketing collateral. Universal catalog brings together the <a href="/dataplex/docs/catalog-overview">data catalog capabilities of Dataplex Catalog</a> and the <a href="/bigquery/docs/about-bqms">runtime metastore capabilities of BigQuery metastore</a>. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-governance">Introduction to data governance in BigQuery</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>Updated pricing, packaging, and setup guidance is now available for <a href="/gemini/docs/bigquery/set-up-gemini">Gemini in BigQuery</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the Apache Arrow format to <a href="/bigquery/docs/supported-data-types#supported-apache-arrow-data-types">stream data to BigQuery with the Storage Write API</a>. This feature is available in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p><em>Analytics Hub</em> has been renamed <a href="/bigquery/docs/analytics-hub-introduction"><em>BigQuery sharing</em></a>. You'll see this new name in the documentation set and the marketing collateral. The product functionality and endpoints remain the same. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-governance">Introduction to data governance in BigQuery</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now combine raster and vector data with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/geography_functions#st_regionstats"><code>ST_REGIONSTATS</code> geography function</a> to perform geospatial analysis in BigQuery. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/raster-data">Work with raster data</a> and try the tutorial that shows you how to <a href="/bigquery/docs/raster-tutorial-weather">use raster data to analyze global temperature by country</a>. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_08_2025">April 08, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/bqms-manage-resources">create, view, modify, and delete Apache Iceberg resources in BigQuery metastore</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now <a href="/bigquery/docs/bqms-use-dataproc#connect-bigquery-flink">connect BigQuery metastore to Apache Flink</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML now offers a built-in <a href="/bigquery/docs/timesfm-model">TimesFM univariate time series forecasting model</a> that implements Google Research's open source TimesFM model. You can use BigQuery ML's built-in TimesFM model with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-forecast"><code>AI.FORECAST</code> function</a> to perform forecasting without having to create and train your own model. This lets you avoid the need for model management.</p>

<p>To try using a TimesFM model with the <code>AI.FORECAST</code> function, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/timesfm-time-series-forecasting-tutorial">Forecast a time series with a TimesFM univariate model</a>.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_07_2025">April 07, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now create <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model">remote models</a> in BigQuery ML based on <a href="/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/partner-models/llama">Llama</a> and <a href="/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/partner-models/mistral">Mistral AI</a> models in Vertex AI.</p>

<p>Use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-text"><code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a> with these remote models to perform generative natural language tasks for text stored in BigQuery tables. Try this feature with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-text">Generate text by using the <code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a> tutorial.</p>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>An updated version of <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/odbc-jdbc-drivers#current_jdbc_driver">JDBC driver for BigQuery</a> is now available.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-introduction">BigQuery data preparation</a> is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA). It offers AI-powered suggestions from Gemini for data cleansing, transformation, and enrichment. BigQuery supports visual data preparation pipelines and pipeline scheduling with Dataform.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/materialized-views-use#smart_tuning">Smart-tuning</a> is now supported for <a href="/bigquery/docs/materialized-views-intro">materialized views</a> when they are in the same project as one of their base tables, or when they are in the project running the query. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery ML now uses dynamic token-based batching for <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-embedding">embedding generation</a> requests. Dynamic token-based batching puts as many rows as possible into one request. This change boosts per-request utilization and improves scalability for any <a href="/bigquery/quotas#cloud_ai_service_functions">queries per minute (QPM) quota</a>. Actual performance varies based on the embedding content length, with an average 10x improvement.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_04_2025">April 04, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML now supports the following <a href="/bigquery/docs/generative-ai-overview#generative_ai_functions">generative AI functions</a>, which let you analyze text using a Vertex AI Gemini model. The function output includes a response that matches the type in the function name:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate"><code>AI.GENERATE</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-bool"><code>AI.GENERATE_BOOL</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-int"><code>AI.GENERATE_INT</code></a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-ai-generate-double"><code>AI.GENERATE_DOUBLE</code></a></li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="April_03_2025">April 03, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="https://cloud.google.com/bigquery/docs/migration-assessment">BigQuery migration assessment</a> now includes support for Amazon Redshift Serverless. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages"> preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now generate structured data by using BigQuery ML's <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-table"><code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code> function</a> with Gemini 1.5 Pro, Gemini 1.5 Flash, and Gemini 2.0 Flash models. You can use the <code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code> function's <code>output_schema</code> argument to more easily format the model's response. The <code>output_schema</code> argument lets you specify a SQL schema for formatting, similar to the schema used in the <code>CREATE TABLE</code> statement. By creating structured output, you can more easily convert the function output into a BigQuery table.</p>

<p>Try this feature with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-table">Generate structured data by using the <code>AI.GENERATE_TABLE</code> function</a> tutorial.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>

<h2 id="April_01_2025">April 01, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can use a <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis"><code>CREATE MODEL</code> statement</a> to create a <a href="/bigquery/docs/contribution-analysis">contribution analysis</a> model in BigQuery ML. The <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis#top_k_insights_by_apriori_support"><code>top_k_insights_by_apriori_support</code></a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis#pruning_method"><code>pruning_method model</code> options</a> are now supported. You can use a contribution analysis model with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-get-insights"><code>ML.GET_INSIGHTS</code> function</a> to generate insights about changes to key metrics in your multi-dimensional data. The following metric types are supported:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis#use_a_summable_metric">Summable metric</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis#use_a_summable_ratio_metric">Summable ratio metric</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-contribution-analysis#use_a_summable_by_category_metric">Summable by category metric</a></li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is <a href="//products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>

<h2 id="March_25_2025">March 25, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>BigQuery ML now supports <a href="/bigquery/docs/model-monitoring-overview#monitoring_visualization">visualization of model monitoring metrics</a>. This feature lets you use charts and graphs to <a href="/vertex-ai/docs/model-monitoring/run-monitoring-job#analyze_monitoring_job_results">analyze model monitoring function output</a>. The following functions support metric visualization:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-validate-data-skew"><code>ML.VALIDATE_DATA_SKEW</code></a>: compute the statistics for a set of serving data, and then compare them to the statistics for the data used to train a BigQuery ML model in order to identify anomalous differences between the two data sets.</li>
<li>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-validate-data-drift"><code>ML.VALIDATE_DATA_DRIFT</code></a>: compute and compare the statistics for two sets of serving data in order to identify anomalous differences between the two data sets.</li>
</ul>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>

<section><h3 id="node.js_4">Node.js</h3>
<h4 id="793_2025-03-17">
<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/nodejs-bigquery/compare/v7.9.2...v7.9.3">7.9.3</a> (2025-03-17)</h4>

This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>

This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/kll_functions">KLL quantile functions</a> to efficiently compute approximate quantiles. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_20_2025">March 20, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now create <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model">remote models</a> in BigQuery ML based on the <a href="/vertex-ai/generative-ai/docs/partner-models/use-claude">Anthropic Claude model</a> in Vertex AI.</p>

<p>Use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-text"><code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a> with these remote models to perform generative natural language tasks for text stored in BigQuery tables. Try this feature with the <a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-text">Generate text by using the <code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a> tutorial.</p>

<p>You can also evaluate Claude models by using the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-evaluate"><code>ML.EVALUATE</code> function</a>.</p>

<p>This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>You can now use <a href="/bigquery/docs/repository-intro">repositories</a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/workspaces-intro">workspaces</a> in BigQuery to perform version control.</p>

<p>Repositories perform version control on files by using Git to record changes and manage file versions. You can use workspaces within repositories to edit the code stored in the repository.</p>

<p>You can have a repository use Git directly on BigQuery, or you can <a href="/bigquery/docs/repositories#connect-third-party">connect a repository to a third-party Git provider</a>.</p>

<p>This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>BigQuery workflows have been renamed to BigQuery pipelines in the Google Cloud console. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/workflows-introduction">Introduction to BigQuery pipelines</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="March_17_2025">March 17, 2025</h2>

This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>

This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now create an <a href="/bigquery/docs/spanner-external-datasets">external dataset</a> in BigQuery that links to an existing database in <a href="/spanner/docs">Spanner</a>. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>

    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use the <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/query-syntax#by_name_or_corresponding"><code>BY NAME</code> and <code>CORRESPONDING</code> modifiers</a> with set operations to match columns by name instead of by position. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div>
<p>The BigQuery ML <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-bucketize"><code>ML.BUCKETIZE</code></a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-quantile-bucketize"><code>ML.QUANTILE_BUCKETIZE</code></a> functions now support formatting of the function output. You can use the <code>output_format</code> argument to format the function output as one of the following:</p>

<ul>
<li>A string in the format <code>bin_&lt;bucket_index&gt;</code>
</li>
<li>A string in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Interval_(mathematics)">interval notation</a>
</li>
<li>A JSON-formatted string</li>
</ul>
</div>
    </div>

    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now set <a href="/bigquery/docs/conditions">conditional IAM access on BigQuery datasets</a> with access control lists (ACLs). This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The following BigQuery ML generative AI features are now available:</p>

<ul>
<li>Creating a
<a href="//bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open">remote model</a>
based on an
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-remote-model-open">open model from Vertex Model Garden or Hugging Face that is deployed to Vertex AI</a>.
Options include Llama, Gemma, and other leading open text generation models.</li>
<li>Using the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-generate-text"><code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a>
with this remote model to perform a broad range of generative AI tasks.</li>
<li>Using the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-evaluate"><code>ML.EVALUATE</code> function</a>
to evaluate the remote model.</li>
</ul>

<p>Try these features with the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-text">Generate text by using the <code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a>
how-to topic and the<br>
<a href="/bigquery/docs/generate-text-tutorial-gemma">Generate text by using a Gemma open model and the <code>ML.GENERATE_TEXT</code> function</a>
tutorial.</p>

<p>These features are
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">generally available</a>
(GA).</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-announcement">Announcement</span>
      <div><p>We previously communicated that after January 27, 2025, a purchase would be required to use <a href="https://cloud.google.com/gemini/docs/bigquery/overview">Gemini in BigQuery features</a>. We are temporarily delaying enforcement of these procurement methods, and no purchase is required at this time. For more information, see <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/gemini/pricing">Gemini for Google Cloud pricing</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_22_2025">January 22, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p><a href="/bigquery/docs/about-bqms">BigQuery metastore</a> lets you access and manage metadata from a variety of processing engines, including BigQuery and Apache Spark. BigQuery metastore supports BigQuery tables and open formats such as Apache Iceberg. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_21_2025">January 21, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can use natural language to <a href="/bigquery/docs/data-prep-get-suggestions">prepare data with Gemini in BigQuery</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>In BigQuery ML, you can now evaluate Anthropic Claude models by using the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-evaluate"><code>ML.EVALUATE</code> function</a>.
<a href="/bigquery/quotas#cloud_ai_service_functions">The quotas</a>
for use of Anthropic Claude models in BigQuery ML have also been brought into
parity with Vertex AI quotas.</p>

<p>This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>Data preparation in BigQuery lets you test data preparations you're developing before you deploy and schedule runs in production. For more information, see <a href="/bigquery/docs/orchestrate-data-preparations#develop">Develop a data preparation</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_20_2025">January 20, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-libraries">Libraries</span>
      <div><devsite-selector><div class="ds-selector-tabs">
<section><h3 id="python_11">Python</h3>
<h4 id="3280_2025-01-15_-_yanked">
<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/compare/v3.27.0...v3.28.0">3.28.0</a> (2025-01-15) - YANKED</h4>

<h4 id="reason_this_release_was_yanked">Reason this release was yanked:</h4>

<p>This turned out to be incompatible with <a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery-pandas">pandas-gbq</a>. For more details, see <a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery-pandas/issues/854">issue</a>.</p>

<h5 id="features_2">Features</h5>

<ul>
<li>Add property for <code>allowNonIncrementalDefinition</code> for materialized view (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2084">#2084</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/3359ef37b90243bea2d9e68bb996fe5d736f304c">3359ef3</a>)</li>
<li>Add property for maxStaleness in table definitions (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2087">#2087</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/729322c2288a30464f2f135ba18b9c4aa7d2f0da">729322c</a>)</li>
<li>Add type hints to Client (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2044">#2044</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/40529de923e25c41c6728c121b9c82a042967ada">40529de</a>)</li>
<li>Adds ExternalCatalogDatasetOptions and tests (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2111">#2111</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/b929a900d49e2c15897134209ed9de5fc7f238cd">b929a90</a>)</li>
<li>Adds ForeignTypeInfo class and tests (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2110">#2110</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/55ca63c23fcb56573e2de67e4f7899939628c4a1">55ca63c</a>)</li>

<li>Resource tags in dataset (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/issues/2090">#2090</a>) (<a href="https://github.com/googleapis/python-bigquery/commit/3e130166f43dcc06704fe90edf9068dfd44842a6">3e13016</a>)</li>

</ul>

    </div>
<h2 id="January_17_2025">January 17, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>In the <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#navigation_menu">navigation menu</a>, you can now go to the <strong>Settings</strong> page to set default settings that are applied when you start a session in BigQuery Studio. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>The BigQuery Data Transfer Service can now transfer data from the following data sources:</p>

<ul>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/mysql-transfer">MySQL</a></li>
<li><a href="/bigquery/docs/postgresql-transfer">PostgreSQL</a></li>
</ul>

<p>Transfers from these data sources are supported in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">Preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_16_2025">January 16, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>The <a href="/bigquery/docs/migration-assessment">BigQuery migration assessment for Oracle</a> now includes a total cost of ownership (TCO) calculator that provides an estimation of compute and storage costs for migrating your Oracle data warehouse to BigQuery. This feature is in <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>We have rearranged the <a href="/bigquery/docs/bigquery-web-ui#navigation_menu">navigation menu</a> into new categories. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_13_2025">January 13, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div><p>You can now use BigQuery Omni Virtual Private Cloud (VPC) allowlists to restrict access to <a href="/bigquery/docs/omni-aws-create-external-table#allow-vpc">AWS S3 buckets</a> and <a href="/bigquery/docs/omni-azure-create-external-table#allow-vpc">Azure Blob Storage</a> from specific BigQuery Omni VPCs. This feature is <a href="https://cloud.google.com/products#product-launch-stages">generally available</a> (GA).</p></div>
    </div>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-feature">Feature</span>
      <div>
<p>In BigQuery ML, you can now forecast multiple time series at once by using the
new
<a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/standard-sql/bigqueryml-syntax-create-multivariate-time-series#time_series_id_col"><code>TIME_SERIES_ID_COL</code> option</a>
that is available in <code>ARIMA_PLUS_XREG</code> multivariate time series models. Try this
feature with the
<a href="/bigquery/docs/arima-plus-xreg-multiple-time-series-forecasting-tutorial">Forecast multiple time series with a multivariate model</a>
tutorial.</p>

<p>This feature is in
<a href="https://cloud.google.com/products/#product-launch-stages">preview</a>.</p>
</div>
    </div>
<h2 id="January_02_2025">January 02, 2025</h2>
    <div class="devsite-release-note">
      <span class="devsite-label devsite-label-release-changed">Change</span>
      <div><p>An updated version of <a href="/bigquery/docs/reference/odbc-jdbc-drivers#current_jdbc_driver">JDBC driver for BigQuery</a> is now available.</p></div>
    </div>



      
    </section>
